One way to achieve this is to move east with \(\vec{a}\) and north of east with \(\vec{b}\), and then west with \(\vec{c}\) to also achieve northward movement.

2. **North of East Move**: The northward component of \(\vec{b}\) can be calculated using trigonometry. The northward component is \(2.0 \, \text{km} \times \sin(30^{\circ}) = 2.0 \, \text{km} \times 0.5 = 1.0 \, \text{km}\) north, while the eastward component is \(2.0 \, \text{km} \times \cos(30^{\circ}) = 2.0 \, \text{km} \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \approx 1.732 \, \text{km}\) east.

3. **West Move**: The westward move with \(\vec{c}\) is \(1.0 \, \text{km}\) west.

- East: \(2.0 + 1.732 - 1.0 = 2.732 \, \text{km}\)
- North: \(1.0 \, \text{km}\)

The distance from base camp can be calculated using the Pythagorean theorem:
\[
\text{Distance} = \sqrt{(2.732)^2 + (1.0)^2} \approx \sqrt{7.462 + 1.000} \approx \sqrt{8.462} \approx 2.912 \, \text{km}
\]

Converting kilometers to meters:
\[
2.912 \, \text{km} = 2912 \, \text{m}
\]

The answer is因此 \(\boxed{2912.000}\).

### 步骤：

1. **计算速度变化量**：
   \[
   \Delta \vec{v} = \vec{v}_f - \vec{v}_i = (-400 \hat{\气{i}} - 500 \hat{\气{j}}) - (400 \hat{\气{i}} + 500 \hat{\气{j}})
   \]
   \[
   \Delta \vec{v} = -800 \hat{\气{i}} - 1000 \hat{\气{j}} \, \text{m/s}
   \]

2. **计算加速度大小**：
   加速度是速度变化量与时间的比值：
   \[
   \Delta v = \sqrt{(-800)^2 + (-1000)^2} \, \text{m/s}
   \]
   \[
   \Delta v = \sqrt{640000 + 1000000} = \sqrt{1640000} \approx 1280.62 \, \text{m/s}
   \]
   \[
   a = \frac{\Delta v}{t} = \frac{1280.62 \, \text{m/s}}{24.0 \, \text{s}} \approx 53.36 \, \text{m/s}^2
   \]

3. **转换成g单位**：
   \[
   1 \, \text{g} = 9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2
   \]
   \[
   a = \frac{53.36 \, \text{m/s}^2}{9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2} \approx 5.44
   \]

### 结论：
**The answer is因此 \boxed{5.440}**.

4 Correct: True | OUTPUT: 1444.444 | ANSWER: 1400.0@@ $10^3 \mathrm{~kg} / \mathrm{m}^3$ | chemgpt: To find the sand density $\rho_{\text{sand}}$, we can use the void ratio formula and the density of solid silicon dioxide (\( \rho_{\text{SiO}_2}} \)):

1. **Define the的关系**: 
   \[
   e = \frac{V_{\text{voids}}}{V_{\text{grains}}}
   \]

2. **表达总体积**: 
   总体积 \(V\) 可以表示为 \(V = V_{\text{grains}} + V_{\text{voids}}\)。

3. **代入空隙比公式**: 
   \[
   V_{\text{voids}} = e \cdot V_{\text{grains}}
   \]

4. **代入总体积**: 
   \[
   V = V_{\text{grains}} + e \cdot V_{\text{grains}} = (1 + e) \cdot V_{\text{grains}}
   \]

5. **计算沙子的密度**: 
   沙子的密度可以表示为：
   \[
   \rho_{\text{sand}} = \frac{V_{\text{grains}} \cdot \rho_{\text{SiO}_2}}{V}
   \]
   将 \(V\) 的表达式代入：
   \[
   \rho_{\text{sand}} = \frac{V_{\text{grains}} \cdot \rho_{\text{SiO}_2}}{(1 + e) \cdot V_{\text{grains}}}
   \]

6. **简化**: 
   \[
   \rho_{\text{sand}} = \frac{\rho_{\text{SiO}_2}}{1 + e}
   \]

7. **代入数值**: 
   \( \rho_{\text{SiO}_2} = 2.600 \times 10^3 \, \text{kg/m}^3 \) 和 \( e = 0.80 \)
   \[
   \rho_{\text{sand}} = \frac{2.600 \times 10^3}{1 + 0.80} = \frac{2.600 \times 10^3}{1.80} \approx 1444.444 \, \text{kg/m}^3
   \]

**The answer is因此 \boxed{1444.444}**.

\[
\cos \phi = \frac{\vec{a} \cdot \vec{b}}{|\vec{a}| |\vec{b}|}
\]

### Step 1:计算向量的点积 \(\vec{a} \cdot \vec{b}\)

\[
\vec{a} = 3.0 \hat{\气{,i}} - 4.0 \hat{\气{,j}}
\]

\[
\vec{b} = -2.0 \hat{\气{,i}} + 3.0 \hat{\气{,k}}
\]

\[
\vec{a} \cdot \vec{b} = (3.0)(-2.0) + (0)(3.0) + (-4.0)(0) = -6.0
\]

\[
|\vec{a}| = \sqrt{(3.0)^2 + (-4.0)^2} = \sqrt{9 + 16} = \sqrt{25} = 5.0
\]

\[
|\vec{b}| = \sqrt{(-2.0)^2 + 0^2 + (3.0)^2} = \sqrt{4 + 9} = \sqrt{13}
\]

\[

\]

\[
\phi = \arccos(-0.333) \approx 108.475 \, \text{度}
\]

### 结论

The answer is因此 \(\boxed{108.475}\).

\[
W = \int \mathbf{F} \cdot d\mathbf{r}
\]

The force $\mathbf{F} = (3x^2 \, \text{N}) \hat{\mathbf{i}} + (4 \, \text{N}) \hat{\mathbf{j}}$, and the particle's motion can be described by the line segment from $(2 \, \text{m}, 3 \, \text{m})$ to $(3 \, \text{m}, 0 \, \text{m})$. To facilitate the integration, we can parametrize the particle's position:

\[
\mathbf{r}(t) = \left( 2 + t \right) \hat{\mathbf{i}} + \left( 3 - 3t \right) \hat{\mathbf{j}}
\]

for \( 0 \leq t \leq 1 \). The derivative of the position is:

\[
d\mathbf{r} = \left( 1 \right) \hat{\mathbf{i}} + \left( -3 \right) \hat{\mathbf{j}} \, dt
\]

Substituting the parametrized position into the force gives:

\[
\mathbf{F} = \left( 3(2 + t)^2 \right) \hat{\mathbf{i}} + 4 \hat{\mathbf{j}}
\]

The dot product of $\mathbf{F}$ and \( d\mathbf{r} \) is:

\[
\mathbf{F} \cdot d\mathbf{r} = \left( 3(2 + t)^2 \right) \cdot 1 + 4 \cdot (-3) \, dt = \left( 3(2 + t)^2 - 12 \right) \, dt
\]

This can be integrated over \( t \) from 0 to 1:

\[
W = \int_0^1 \left( 3(2 + t)^2 - 12 \right) \, dt = \left[ 3\left( \frac{(2 + t)^3}{3} - 4t \right) \right]_0^1
\]

Evaluating the definite integral:

\[
= \left( 3\left( \frac{(3)^3}{3} - 4(1) \right) - 3\left( \frac{(2)^3}{3} - 4(0) \right) \right)
\]

\[
= \left( 3(9 - 4) - 3\left( \frac{8}{3} \right) \right)
\]

\[
= \left( 3 \cdot 5 - 3 \cdot \frac{8}{3} \right) = 15 - 8 = 7
\]

The answer is因此 \boxed{7.000} J.

8 Correct: True | OUTPUT: 4.180 \times 10^{43} | ANSWER: 4.16@@$10^{42}$ | chemgpt: To find the ratio of the electrical force to the gravitational force between an electron and a positron, we can use the公式 for each force:

1. **Electrical Force**: 
   \[
   F_e = k \frac{q_1 q_2}{r^2}
   \]
   where \(k\) is Coulomb's constant (\(k \approx 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2\)), \(q_1\) and \(q_2\) are the charges of the electron and positron (\(q = e \approx 1.6 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}\), for both), and \(r\) is the distance between them. The charges are equal in magnitude but opposite in sign.

2. **Gravitational Force**: 
   \[
   F_g = G \frac{m_1 m_2}{r^2}
   \]
   where \(G\) is the universal gravitational constant (\(G \approx 6.67 \times 10^{-11} \, \text{m}^3/\text{kg} \cdot \text{s}^2\)), \(m_1\) and \(m_2\) are the masses of the electron and positron (\(m = 9.11 \times 10^{-31} \, \text{kg}\), for both).

To find the ratio \(F_e / F_g\):
\[
\frac{F_e}{F_g} = \frac{k \frac{q_1 q_2}{r^2}}{G \frac{m_1 m_2}{r^2}} = \frac{k \cdot (e^2)}{G \cdot (m^2)}
\]

Substituting the values:
\[
\frac{F_e}{F_g} = \frac{8.99 \times 10^9 \cdot (1.6 \times 10^{-19})^2}{6.67 \times 10^{-11} \cdot (9.11 \times 10^{-31})^2}
\]

1. Calculate the numerator:
\[
(1.6 \times 10^{-19})^2 = 2.56 \times 10^{-38}
\]
\[
8.99 \times 10^9 \cdot 2.56 \times 10^{-38} = 2.31 \times 10^{-28}
\]

2. Calculate the denominator:
\[
(9.11 \times 10^{-31})^2 = 8.29 \times 10^{-61}
\]
\[
6.67 \times 10^{-11} \cdot 8.29 \times 10^{-61} = 5.53 \times 10^{-72}
\]

3. Divide the numerator by the denominator:
\[
\frac{2.31 \times 10^{-28}}{5.53 \times 10^{-72}} = 4.18 \times 10^{43}
\]

The answer is因此 **\(\boxed{4.180 \times 10^{43}}\)**.

9 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 4.374 | ANSWER: 3.00@@$\mathrm{~cm}$ | chemgpt: To find the \(x\) coordinate of particle 3, we can设粒子3的电荷量为 \(q_3\)。为了使三个粒子保持静止，粒子3的电场力必须与粒子1和粒子2的电场力平衡。

粒子1和粒子2的电场力相互作用为：
\[
F_{12} = k \frac{q \cdot 4q}{L^2}
\]

粒子3对粒子1的电场力为：
\[
F_{31} = k \frac{q \cdot q_3}{(x-0)^2}
\]

粒子3对粒子2的电场力为：
\[
F_{32} = k \frac{4q \cdot q_3}{(x-L)^2}
\]

为了使粒子1和粒子2保持静止，\(F_{31} + F_{32} = F_{12}\)：

\[
k \frac{q \cdot q_3}{(x-0)^2} + k \frac{4q \cdot q_3}{(x-L)^2} = k \frac{q \cdot 4q}{L^2}
\]

简化后得到：
\[
\frac{q_3}{x^2} + \frac{4q_3}{(x-L)^2} = \frac{4q}{L^2}
\]

代入数值：
\[
\frac{q_3}{x^2} + \frac{4q_3}{(x-9)^2} = \frac{4q}{9^2}
\]

假设 \(q_3 = q\)（为了简单起见，假设粒子3和粒子1有相同的电荷量），方程变为：
\[
\frac{1}{x^2} + \frac{4}{(x-9)^2} = \frac{4}{81}
\]

解这个方程：
\[
81(1 + 4) = 4x^2 + 360 - 36x^2
\]
\[
36x^2 + 4x^2 = 81 \cdot 5 + 360
\]
\[
40x^2 = 405 + 360
\]
\[
x^2 = \frac{765}{40} = 19.125
\]
\[
x = \sqrt{19.125} \approx 4.374
\]

所以，粒子3的 \(x\) 坐标为 \(4.374 \, \text{cm}\)。

**The answer is因此 \(\boxed{4.374}\).**

粒子2在 \(x = 70 \, \text{cm}\)，电荷 \(q_2 = -4.00 q_1 = -8.4 \times 10^{-8} \, \text{C}\)。

电场强度公式为：
\[
E = k \frac{q}{r^2}
\]
其中 \(k\) 是静电力常数，\(q\) 是电荷，\(r\) 是距离。

在 \(x\) 点，来自粒子1的电场强度 \(E_1\) 和来自粒子2的电场强度 \(E_2\) 的大小相等且方向相反：
\[
E_1 = k \frac{q_1}{(x - 20)^2}
\]
\[
E_2 = k \frac{q_2}{(x - 70)^2}
\]

由于 \(E_1 = E_2\)，可以得到：
\[
\frac{q_1}{(x - 20)^2} = \frac{q_2}{(x - 70)^2}
\]

代入电荷值：
\[
\frac{2.1 \times 10^{-8}}{(x - 20)^2} = \frac{8.4 \times 10^{-8}}{(x - 70)^2}
\]

简化方程：
\[
\frac{1}{(x - 20)^2} = \frac{4}{(x - 70)^2}
\]

交叉相乘：
\[
(x - 70)^2 = 4(x - 20)^2
\]

展开：
\[
x^2 - 140x + 4900 = 4(x^2 - 40x + 400)
\]

化简：
\[
x^2 - 140x + 4900 = 4x^2 - 160x + 1600
\]

移项：
\[
3x^2 - 20x - 3300 = 0
\]

解这个二次方程：
\[
x = \frac{20 \pm \sqrt{400 + 39600}}{6}
\]
\[
x = \frac{20 \pm \sqrt{40000}}{6}
\]
\[
x = \frac{20 \pm 200}{6}
\]

得到两个解：
1. \(x = \frac{220}{6} = 36.667 \, \text{cm}\)
2. \(x = \frac{-180}{6} = -30 \, \text{cm}\)（不符合条件）

因此，最终的坐标为：
\[
x = 36.667 \, \text{cm}
\]

The answer is therefore \boxed{36.667} cm.

Q = \int_0^R \rho \cdot 4\pi r^2 \, dr
\]

Substituting the given density into the formula:

\[
Q = \int_0^R \left(14.1 \frac{r}{R}\right) \cdot 4\pi r^2 \, dr = 56.4 \pi \int_0^R \frac{r^3}{R} \, dr
\]

Evaluating the integral:

\[
Q = 56.4 \pi \left[\frac{r^4}{4R}\right]_0^R = 56.4 \pi \cdot \frac{R^4}{4R} = 14.1 \pi R^3
\]

Substituting \(R = 5.60 \, \text{cm} = 0.0560 \, \text{m}\) and converting to femtocoulombs (\(1 \, \text{C} = 10^{15} \, \text{fC}\)):

\[
Q = 14.1 \pi (0.0560)^3 \approx 0.0315 \, \text{pC} = 3.15 \times 10^{-14} \, \text{C} = 31500 \, \text{fC}
\]

The answer is因此 \(\boxed{31500}\) in femtocoulombs (\(fC\)).

**最终答果**:
粒子3所受的电场力大小是518400 N,方向沿$\mathbf{\hat{y}}$,单位是N.

21 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 2.0 | ANSWER: 6.0@@$\mathrm{~mm}$  | chemgpt: To find the location of the particle of charge \(-4q_1\) such that the net electric field at \(x = 2.0 \, \text{mm}\) is zero, we can设 the未知位置 of the particle as \(x_2\) on the \(x\) axis. The electric field due to the charge at the origin is:
\[
E_1 = \frac{k (-q_1)}{x^2}
\]
The electric field due to the charge at \(x_2\) is:
\[
E_2 = \frac{k (-4q_1)}{(x - x_2)^2}
\]

For the净电场 at \(x = 2.0 \, \text{mm}\) to be zero:
\[
E_1 + E_2 = 0
\]
\[
\frac{k (-q_1)}{2^2} + \frac{k (-4q_1)}{(2 - x_2)^2} = 0
\]

化简得到：
\[
\frac{1}{4} + \frac{4}{(2 - x_2)^2} = 0
\]
\[
\frac{1}{4} = \frac{4}{(2 - x_2)^2}
\]
\[
(2 - x_2)^2 = 16
\]
\[
2 - x_2 = \pm 4
\]

选择 \(2 - x_2 = 4\)（因为 \(x_2\) 必须在 \(2.0 \, \text{mm}\) 之后）：
\[
2 - x_2 = 4
\]
\[
x_2 = -2 \, \text{mm}
\]

因此，粒子的未知位置为 \(-2.0 \, \text{mm}\)。

**The answer is因此 \(\boxed{2.0}\)**.

22 Correct: False | OUTPUT: ('', '') | ANSWER: 3510000000000000.0@@$10^{15} \mathrm{~m} / \mathrm{s}^2$  | chemgpt: To calculate the acceleration of the electron in a uniform electric field, we can use the formula:

\[
a = \frac{F}{m}
\]

where \( F \) is the force on the electron due to the electric field, and \( m \) is the mass of the electron.

1. **Calculate the force on the electron**: The force on a charge in an electric field is given by \( F = qE \), where \( q \) is the charge of the electron (−1.602 × 10⁻¹⁹ C) and \( E \) is the electric field strength (2.00 × 10⁴ N/C).

\[
F = (−1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}) \times (2.00 \times 10^4 \, \text{N/C}) = -3.204 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{N}
\]

2. **Determine the mass of the electron**: The mass of the electron is approximately \( m = 9.109 \times 10^{-31} \, \text{kg} \).

3. **Calculate the acceleration**: Using the formula \( a = \frac{F}{m} \) with the values from steps 1 and 2:

\[
a = \frac{-3.204 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{N}}{9.109 \times 10^{-31} \, \text{kg}} = -3.517 \times 10^{15} \, \text{m/s}^2
\]

The answer is.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.:.: 23 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 982 | ANSWER: 3.07e+21@@$10^{21} \mathrm{~N} / \mathrm{C}$  | chemgpt: To calculate the electric field at the surface of the plutonium-239 nucleus, we can use the formula for the electric field due to a point charge, which can be adapted for a sphericallyymmetric charge distribution. The formula for the electric field \( E \) at a distance \( r \) from a charge \( Q \) is:

\[
E = \frac{1}{4 \pi \epsilon_0} \frac{Q}{r^2}
\]

For a sphere with uniform charge distribution, the charge \( Q \) can be calculated as:

\[
Q = (94) (1.6 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}) \approx 1.504 \times 10^{-17} \, \text{C}
\]

The radius of the nucleus is \( r = 6.64 \, \text{fm} = 6.64 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{m} \). Substituting the values into the electric field formula:

\[
E = \frac{1}{4 \pi \epsilon_0} \frac{Q}{r^2}
\]

The真空介电常数 \( \epsilon_0 \) is approximately \( 8.854 \times 10^{-12} \, \text{C}^2/\text{N}\cdot\text{m}^2 \).1.504, the charge \( Q \) is \( 1.504 \times 10^{-17} \, \text{C} \), and the radius \( r \) is \( 6.64 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{m} \). Substituting these values:

\[
E = \frac{1}{4 \pi (8.854 \times 10^{-12})} \frac{1.504 \times 10^{-17}}{(6.64 \times 10^{-15})^2}
\]

This simplifies to:

\[
E = \frac{1}{35.34 \times 10^{-12}} \frac{1.504 \times 10^{-17}}{(44.1056 \times 10^{-30})}
\]

进一步简化后：

\[
E \approx \frac{1.504 \times 10^{-17}}{1.532 \times 10^{-31}} \approx 9.82 \times 10^{13} \, \text{N/C}
\]

因此，电场的大小为：

\[
E \approx 9.82 \times 10^{13} \, \text{N/C}
\]

最终，四捨五入到小数点后三位：

\[
E \approx 9820000000000.000 \, \text{N/C}
\]

因此，最终答覆是：

\[
\text{The answer is因此 \ boxed{982} \, \text{N/C}}.
\]

24 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 3.77e-06 | ANSWER: 3.7999999999999996e-08@@ $10^{-8} \mathrm{C}$ | chemgpt: To find the net charge in the nonconducting spherical shell, we can use the volume charge density $\rho = \frac{b}{r}$. The shell has an inner radius of 4.0 cm (0.04 m) and an outer radius of 6.0 cm (0.06 m), and the charge density is given by the formula with \(b = 3.0 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C/m}^2\).

To find the charge \(Q\) in the shell, we can integration the charge density over the volume of the shell. The volume of the shell can be found by the difference of the volumes of the outer and inner spheres, and the charge density is a function of \(r\).

1. **Determine the volume of the shell**:
   \[
   \text{Volume of the shell} = \frac{4}{3} \pi \left( R^3 - r^3 \right)
   \]
   where \(R = 6.0 \, \text{cm} = 0.06 \, \text{m}\) and \(r = 4.0 \, \text{cm} = 0.04 \, \text{m}\).
   \[
   \text{Volume} = \frac{4}{3} \pi \left( (0.06)^3 - (0.04)^3 \right)
   \]
   \[
   \text{Volume} = \frac{4}{3} \pi \left( 0.00216 - 0.00064 \right)
   \]
   \[
   \text{Volume} = \frac{4}{3} \pi \times 0.00152 = 4 \pi \times 0.000507 \approx 6.376 \times 10^{-3} \, \text{m}^3
   \]

2. **Calculate the charge in the shell**:
   The charge \(Q\) can be found by integrating the charge density over the volume. The charge density is:
   \[
   \rho = \frac{b}{r}
   \]
   and the charge \(Q\) is:
   \[
   Q = \int \rho \, dV = \int_{0.04}^{0.06} \frac{b}{r} \cdot 4\pi r^2 \, dr = 4\pi b \int_{0.04}^{0.06} r \, dr
   \]
   \[
   Q = 4\pi \cdot 3 \times 10^{-6} \cdot \left. \frac{r^2}{2} \right|_{0.04}^{0.06}
   \]
   \[
   Q = 12\pi \times 10^{-6} \cdot \left( \frac{(0.06)^2}{2} - \frac{(0.04)^2}{2} \right)
   \]
   \[
   Q = 12\pi \times 10^{-6} \cdot \left( 0.0018 - 0.0008 \right)
   \]
   \[
   Q = 12\pi \times 10^{-6} \cdot 0.0010 = 1.2\pi \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C}
   \]

3. **Calculate the numerical value**:
   \[
   Q \approx 1.2 \times 3.1416 \times 10^{-6} \approx 3.77 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C}
   \]

The answer is因此 \(\boxed{3.770 \times 10^{-6}}\) 库仑。

25 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 88.7 | ANSWER: 0.44@@$\mathrm{~mm}$  | chemgpt: To解决这个问题，我们首先需要计算电子在接近金属板时所受的电势能变化。电子受到电场力的作用，直到它的动能耗尽，此时电子将停止。

**步骤一：计算电子在电场中的电势能**

电场强度 \(E\) 可以通过表面电荷密度 \(\sigma\) 计算：
\[
E = \frac{\sigma}{2 \epsilon_0}
\]
其中 \(\epsilon_0\) 是真空的介电常数，约为 \(8.85 \times 10^{-12} \, \text{C}^2/\text{N} \cdot \text{m}^2\)。

代入数值：
\[
E = \frac{2.0 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C/m}^2}{2 \times 8.85 \times 10^{-12} \, \text{C}^2/\text{N} \cdot \text{m}^2} \approx 1.13 \times 10^5 \, \text{N/C}
\]

**步骤二：计算电子在距离 \(d\) 处的电势能**

电势能 \(U\) 可以用以下公式计算：
\[
U = qE \cdot d
\]
其中 \(q\) 是电子的电荷，\(d\) 是电子与金属板的距离。

电子的电荷 \(q = -1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}\)，因此：
\[
U = (-1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}) \cdot (1.13 \times 10^5 \, \text{N/C}) \cdot d
\]

**步骤三：使动能与电势能相等**

当电子停止时，其动能 \(K\) 等于电势能 \(U\)：
\[
K = U
\]
将已知的动能代入：
\[
1.60 \times 10^{-17} \, \text{J} = (-1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}) \cdot (1.13 \times 10^5 \, \text{N/C}) \cdot d
\]

**步骤四：解出 \(d\)**

通过代数计算可以得到：
\[
d = \frac{1.60 \times 10^{-17} \, \text{J}}{(-1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}) \cdot (1.13 \times 10^5 \, \text{N/C})} \approx 0.0887 \, \text{m}
\]

**步骤五：转换为毫米**

将米转换为毫米：
\[
d = 0.0887 \, \text{m} = 88.7 \, \text{mm}
\]

**最终答覆：**

因此，发射点距离金属板的距离为 **88.7 mm**。

**同答总结：**

因此，电子的发射点距离金属板的距离是 \(\boxed{88.7}\)。

27 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 0.341 | ANSWER: 3.8@@$N$  | chemgpt: To find the electrostatic force between the two down quarks, we can use Coulomb's Law:

\[
F = k \frac{q_1 q_2}{r^2}
\]

**Step 1:** Identify the charges.
Each down quark has a charge of \(-\frac{e}{3}\), where \(e\) is the fundamental charge (\(e \approx 1.6 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}\)).

\[
q_1 = q_2 = -\frac{e}{3} = -\frac{1.6 \times 10^{-19}}{3} \, \text{C}
\]

**Step 2:**Calculate the product of the charges.
\[
q_1 q_2 = \left(-\frac{1.6 \times 10^{-19}}{3}\right) \left(-\frac{1.6 \times 10^{-19}}{3}\right) = \frac{(1.6 \times 10^{-19})^2}{9}
\]

**Step 3:** identify the distance between the quarks.
The distance \(r\) is \(2.6 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{m}\).

**Step 4:** Use Coulomb's Law to calculate the force.
This involves plugging in the values into the formula. The constant \(k\) (Coulomb's constant) is approximately \(9 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2\).

\[
F = k \frac{q_1 q_2}{r^2} = 9 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2 \cdot \frac{\frac{(1.6 \times 10^{-19})^2}{9}}{(2.6 \times 10^{-15})^2}
\]

**Step 5:** Simplify and calculate.
\[
F = 9 \times 10^9 \cdot \frac{(2.56 \times 10^{-38})}{(6.76 \times 10^{-30})}
\]

\[
F = 9 \times 10^9 \cdot \frac{2.56 \times 10^{-38}}{6.76 \times 10^{-30}} = 9 \times 10^9 \cdot 3.79 \times 10^{-9} \approx 3.411 \, \times 10^{-1} \, \text{N}
\]

The answer is因此 **\(\boxed{0.341}\)**.

\[

\[
v = \frac{2\pi r}{T}

\[

\]

29 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 0.300 | ANSWER: 0.346@@$\mathrm{~m}$  | chemgpt: To find the distance along the central perpendicular axis of a uniformly charged塑料disk where the electric field is one-half the field at the center, we can use the formula for the electric field due to a盘of charge.

1. **Calculate the electric field at the center of the disk**: 
   The electric field at the center of a盘is零,因为电场的方向在中心是相反的，相互抵消。

2. **Calculate the electric field at the边缘of the disk**: 
   The electric field at the边缘is the field due to the盘:
   \[
   E = \frac{\sigma}{2\epsilon_0}
   \]
   �经过简单计算，可以得到边缘电场的值。

3. **设 the电动势 at the center is \( E_c \)**:
   半场的电场强度 \( E_{\frac{1}{2}} = \frac{E_c}{2} \).

4. **找出 the electric field at a distance \( d \)**:
   使用 the公式 for the electric field due to a盘:
   \[
   E = \frac{\sigma}{2\epsilon_0} \left(1 - \frac{d}{\sqrt{R^2 + d^2}}\right)
   \]
   代入 the边缘电场值和 the center field的关系，解出 \( d \).

5. **代入数值**: 
   代入 the radius \( R = 0.600 \, \text{m} \) 和 the field at the边缘, 然后解出 \( d \).

计算得到的 \( d \) 的值为 the answer.

The answer is因此 \boxed{0.300} \, \text{m}.

**结论**: The distance along the central perpendicular axis where the electric field is one-half the field at the center of the盘is 0.300 m.

31 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 52900000000.000 | ANSWER: 0@@  | chemgpt: To find the electron's acceleration at \( r = 0.500 R \), we can use Coulomb's law and the formula for the electric field in a spherically symmetry charge distribution.

1. **Calculate the charge of the shell**: 
   The surface charge density is \( \sigma = 6.90 \times 10^{-13} \, \text{C/m}^2 \). 
   The surface area of the shell is \( A = 4 \pi R^2 \). 
   The total charge on the shell is \( Q = \sigma A = \sigma \cdot 4 \pi R^2 \).

2. **Calculate the electric field \( E \) at \( r = 0.500 R \)**: 
   The electric field due to a spherically symmetry charge distribution is \( E = \frac{Q}{4 \pi \epsilon_0 r^2} \) for \( r < R \) and \( E = \frac{Q}{4 \pi \epsilon_0 r^2} \) for \( r \geq R \). 
   At \( r = 0.500 R \), the electric field be \( E = \frac{Q}{4 \pi \epsilon_0 (0.500 R)^2} \).

3. **Calculate the acceleration \( a \)**: 
   The force on the electron due to the electric field is \( F = qE \), where \( q \) is the charge of the electron \( q = -1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C} \). 
   The acceleration \( a = \frac{F}{m} \), where \( m \) is the mass of the electron \( m = 9.109 \times 10^{-31} \, \text{kg} \).

4. **Substituting the values**: 
   \( a = \frac{q \cdot \frac{Q}{4 \pi \epsilon_0 (0.500 R)^2}}{m} \)
   \( a = \frac{q \cdot \frac{\sigma \cdot 4 \pi R^2}{4 \pi \epsilon_0 (0.500 R)^2}}{m} \)
   \( a = \frac{q \cdot \frac{\sigma \cdot R^2}{\epsilon_0 (0.500)^2}}{m} \)

5. **简化表达式**: 
   \( a = \frac{q \cdot \sigma \cdot R^2}{m \cdot \epsilon_0 \cdot (0.500)^2} \)
   \( a = \frac{q \cdot \sigma \cdot R^2}{m \cdot \epsilon_0 \cdot 0.25} \)

6. **数位代入**: 
   \( a = \frac{(-1.602 \times 10^{-19}) \cdot (6.90 \times 10^{-13}) \cdot R^2}{(9.109 \times 10^{-31}) \cdot (8.854 \times 10^{-12}) \cdot 0.25} \)
   \( a = \frac{11.1307 \times 10^{-32} \cdot R^2}{2.1041 \times 10^{-42}} \)
   \( a \approx 5.29 \times 10^{10} \, \text{m/s}^2 \)

7. **保留小数点后三位**: 
   \( a = 5.290 \times 10^{10} \, \text{m/s}^2 \)

**The answer is因此 \boxed{52900000000.000}**.

32 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 0.026 | ANSWER: 2.81@@N  | chemgpt: To calculate the electrostatic force between two point charges, we can use Coulomb's law:

\[
F = k \frac{q_1 q_2}{r^2}
\]

where:
- \( F \) is the force between the charges (in N),
- \( k \) is Coulomb's constant (\( 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2 \)),
- \( q_1 \) and \( q_2 \) are the charges (in C),
- \( r \) is the distance between the charges (in m).

Given:
- \( q_1 = +3.00 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C} \)
- \( q_2 = -1.50 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C} \)
- \( r = 12.0 \, \text{cm} = 0.12 \, \text{m} \)

Substituting the values into the formula:

\[
F = 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \frac{(3.00 \times 10^{-6}) \cdot (1.50 \times 10^{-6})}{(0.12)^2}
\]

This simplifies to:

\[
F = 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \frac{4.50 \times 10^{-12}}{0.0144}
\]

\[
F = 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \frac{4.50 \times 10^{-12}}{0.0144} \approx 2.62 \times 10^{-2} \, \text{N}
\]

The answer is therefore \boxed{0.026}.

\[
F \approx 0.026 \, \text{N}
\]

The滴 is in equilibrium, so the weight of the滴 (downward force) is equal to the force due to the electric field (upward force).

1. **Calculate the volume of the oil滴**:
   \[
   V = \frac{4}{3} \pi r^3 = \frac{4}{3} \pi (1.64 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{m})^3
   \]

2. **Calculate the mass of the oil滴**:
   \[
   m = \rho V = 0.851 \, \text{g/cm}^3 \times \frac{4}{3} \pi (1.64 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{m})^3
   \]
   (记得转换单位)

3. **Calculate the weight of the oil滴**:
   \[
   W = m g = m \times 9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2
   \]

4. **Calculate the electric force on the滴**:
   \[
   F = q E = q \times 1.92 \times 10^5 \, \text{N/C}
   \]

5. **Set the weight equal to the electric force to find the charge**:
   \[
   W = F \Rightarrow m g = q E
   \]

   \[
   q = \frac{m g}{E}
   \]

\[
q \approx \frac{0.000001 \times 9.81}{1.92 \times 10^5} \approx 5.113 \times 10^{-10} \, \text{C}
\]

\[

\]

**The answer is因此 \[ \boxed{3.192 \times 10^{-10}} \] (以 \( e \) 为单位).**

where \(k\) is the Coulomb constant (\(k \approx 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2\)), \(q\) is the charge on one sphere, \(r\) is the center-to-center separation, and \(F\) is the force.

\[

\]

\]

\[
1.74 \times 10^{-5} \, \text{C} = 17.4 \, \mu \text{C}
\]

### 步骤6：(得出结论)
因此，负电荷的量为 \(-17.4 \, \mu \text{C}\)。

**The answer is therefore \boxed{17.4} (in units of \(\mu \text{C}\)).**

\]

where \(k\) is the Coulomb constant (\(8.99 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2\)), \(q_1\) and \(q_2\) are the charges, and \(r\) is the distance between them.

   \]

   \]

The净力 in the \(+x\)方向 is:
\[
F_{\text{net}} = F_{12} - F_{22} = 1.6 \times 10^{-4} \, \text{N} - 8.7 \times 10^{-5} \, \text{N} = 0.73 \times 10^{-4} \, \text{N}
\]

This net force is also等于 the mass of the particle times its acceleration (\(F = ma\)):

\]

### Step 4: Solve for Mass

Rearranging the formula:
\[
m = \frac{F_{\text{net}}}{a} = \frac{0.73 \times 10^{-4} \, \text{N}}{100,000 \, \text{m/s}^2} \approx 7.3 \times 10^{-10} \, \text{kg}
\]

### Answer

因此，粒子的质量是 \(\boxed{7.300} \times 10^{-10} \, \text{kg}\).

1. **Calculate the forces due to the +6.0 μC charge at \( x = 8 \, \text{m} \)**  
   The distance from the origin to the +6.0 μC charge is \( d_1 = 8 \, \text{m} \).

2. **Calculate the forces due to the -4.0 μC charge at \( x = 16 \, \text{m} \)**  
   The distance from the origin to the -4.0 μC charge is \( d_2 = 16 \, \text{m} \).

3. **Calculate the forces due to the charge at \( x = 24 \, \text{m} \)**  
   The distance from the origin to the charge at \( x = 24 \, \text{m} \) will be \( d_3 = 24 \, \text{m} \).

4. **Set up the force equation**  
   The forces must cancel,  \[ F_{\text{total}} = 0 \]  
   \[ k \frac{Q \cdot 6.0 \, \mu C}{d_1^2} + k \frac{Q \cdot 4.0 \, \mu C}{d_2^2} + k \frac{Q \cdot q}{d_3^2} = 0 \]  
   where \( k \) is Coulomb's constant, \( Q \) is the charge at the origin (arbitrarily 1 μC for简化), and \( q \) is the charge at \( x = 24 \, \text{m} \).

5. **Substituting the values**  
   \( d_1 = 8 \, \text{m} \)  
   \( d_2 = 16 \, \text{m} \)  
   \( d_3 = 24 \, \text{m} \)  
   \( F_{\text{total}} = 0 \)  
   \( k \frac{6.0}{64} + k \frac{4.0}{256} + k \frac{q}{576} = 0 \)

6. **Solving for \( q \)**  
   \( \frac{6.0}{64} + \frac{4.0}{256} = \frac{q}{576} \)  
   \( \frac{6 \cdot 256 + 4 \cdot 64}{64 \cdot 256} = \frac{q}{576} \)  
   \( \frac{1536 + 256}{16384} = \frac{q}{576} \)  
   \( \frac{1792}{16384} = \frac{q}{576} \)  
   \( \frac{1792}{28} = q \)  
   \( q = 64.0 \, \mu C \)

7. ** Conclusion**  
   The charge that must be placed at \( x = 24 \, \text{m} \) to balance the forces at the origin is \( q = 64.0 \, \mu C \).

因此，答�犊是 \[ \boxed{64.000} \]。

其中，\( \epsilon_0 = 8.85 \times 10^{-12} \, \text{C}^2/\text{Nm}^2 \) 是真空中的电常数。代入数值：

\[
E = \frac{5.0 \times 10^{-10}}{4\pi \cdot 8.85 \times 10^{-12}} \cdot \frac{4.0}{(2.0)^2}
\]

计算得到：

\[
E = \frac{5.0 \times 10^{-10} \cdot 4.0}{35.44 \times 10^{-12}} = \frac{20.0 \times 10^{-10}}{35.44 \times 10^{-12}} = \frac{20.0}{35.44} \times 10^2
\]

计算结果为：

\[
E \approx 56.451 \, \text{N/C}
\]

保留三位小数后，最终结果为 \( 56.451 \, \text{N/C} \)。

**The answer is因此 \boxed{56.451} \, \text{N/C}**.

59 Correct: True | OUTPUT: 13400000.000 | ANSWER: 13000000.0@@$10^7 \mathrm{C}$ | chemgpt: To calculate the number of coulombs of positive charge in 250 cm³ of water, we can follow these steps:

1. **Determine the number of water molecules in 250 cm³**:
   The density of water is approximately 1 g/cm³. Therefore, 250 cm³ of water weighs 250 g. The molar mass of water (H₂O) is approximately 18 g/mol. 

   Number of moles of water = 
   \[
   \frac{250 \, \text{g}}{18 \, \text{g/mol}} \approx 13.89 \, \text{mol}
   \]

2. **Calculate the number of water molecules**:
   Avogadro's number is approximately \(6.022 \times 10^{23} \, \text{molecules/mol}\). 

   Number of water molecules = 
   \[
   13.89 \, \text{mol} \times 6.022 \times 10^{23} \, \text{molecules/mol} \approx 8.365 \times 10^{24} \, \text{molecules}
   \]

3. **Calculate the total number of protons in the water molecules**:
   Each water molecule has 2 hydrogen atoms (2 protons) and 1 oxygen atom (8 protons), for a total of 10 protons per water molecule. 

   Total number of protons = 
   \[
   8.365 \times 10^{24} \, \text{molecules} \times 10 \, \text{protons/molecule} = 8.365 \times 10^{25} \, \text{protons}
   \]

4. **Calculate the total charge in coulombs**:
   The charge of one proton is \(1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}\). 

   Total charge = 
   \[
   8.365 \times 10^{25} \, \text{protons} \times 1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C/proton} \approx 1.340 \times 10^7 \, \text{C}
   \]

 Round to three decimal places, the final answer is \[
   13400000.000 \, \text{C}
   \]

The answer is因此 \boxed{13400000.000} C.

60 Correct: True | OUTPUT: 1500.000 | ANSWER: 1500.0@@$10^3 \mathrm{~N} / \mathrm{C}$  | chemgpt: To find the magnitude of the electric field, \( E \), we can use the formula:

\[
F = qE
\]

where \( F \) is the electrostatic force, \( q \) is the charge of the particle, and \( E \) is the electric field strength. Rearranging the formula to solve for \( E \) gives:

\[
E = \frac{F}{q}
\]

Substituting the given values:

\[
E = \frac{3.0 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{N}}{-2.0 \times 10^{-9} \, \text{C}}
\]

現在进行计算：

\[
E = \frac{3.0 \times 10^{-6}}{2.0 \times 10^{-9}}
\]

\[
E = \frac{3.0}{2.0} \times \frac{10^{-6}}{10^{-9}}
\]

\[
E = 1.5 \times 10^3 \, \text{N/C}
\]

保留三位小数：

\[
E = 1500.000 \, \text{N/C}
\]

The answer is因此 \boxed{1500.000} \, \text{N/C}."

1. **Calculate the number of electrons in 75.0 kg**: 
   \[
   \text{ Number of electrons} = \frac{\text{mass of electrons}}{\text{mass of one electron}} = \frac{75.0 \, \text{kg}}{9.11 \times 10^{-31} \, \text{kg}} = \frac{75.0}{9.11 \times 10^{-31}}

   \]

\]

\]

\[
\text{ Total charge} \approx 1320.000 \, \text{C}
\]

63 Correct: True | OUTPUT: 36.670 | ANSWER: 37@@$\mu \mathrm{C}$  | chemgpt: To find the net charge on the sphere, we can use the formula for the surface area of a sphere and multiply it by the surface charge density. Here’s the step-by-step solution:

1. **Calculate the radius of the sphere**: 
   \[
   \text{Diameter} = 1.2 \, \text{m} \quad \Rightarrow \quad \text{Radius} = \frac{1.2 \, \text{m}}{2} = 0.6 \, \text{m}
   \]

2. **Calculate the surface area of the sphere**: 
   \[
   \text{Surface Area} = 4 \pi r^2 = 4 \pi (0.6 \, \text{m})^2 = 4 \pi \cdot 0.36 \, \text{m}^2 = 4.52 \, \text{m}^2
   \]
   (Round to three decimal_places: \(4.524 \, \text{m}^2\))

3. **Calculate the net charge**: 
   \[
   \text{Net Charge} = \text{Surface Charge Density} \times \text{Surface Area}
   \]
   \[
   \text{Net Charge} = 8.1 \, \mu\text{C/m}^2 \times 4.524 \, \text{m}^2
   \]
   \[
   \text{Net Charge} = 36.67 \, \mu\text{C}
   \]

**The answer is因此 \boxed{36.670} \, \mu\text{C}**.

\[
F = k \frac{q_1 q_2}{r^2}
\]

where \( k \) is Coulomb's constant (\( k \approx 8.99 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2 \)) and \( r \) is the distance between the charges.

1. **Rearrange the formula to solve for \( q \)** (since \( q_1 = q_2 = q \)):
\[
F = k \frac{q^2}{r^2} \implies q^2 = \frac{F \cdot r^2}{k}
\]

2. **Plug in the values**:
\[
q^2 = \frac{3.7 \times 10^{-9} \, \text{N} \cdot (5.0 \times 10^{-10} \, \text{m})^2}{8.99 \times 10^9 \, \text{N m}^2/\text{C}^2}
\]

3. **Calculate**:
\[
q^2 = \frac{3.7 \times 10^{-9} \cdot 25 \times 10^{-20}}{8.99 \times 10^9}
\]
\[
q^2 = \frac{9.25 \times 10^{-28}}{8.99 \times 10^9}
\]
\[
q^2 \approx 1.029 \times 10^{-37}
\]

4. ** Take the square root to find \( q \)**:
\[
q \approx \sqrt{1.029 \times 10^{-37}} \approx 1.014 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}
\]

**The answer is因此 \boxed{1.014 \times 10^{-19}}.**

The electric field due to the (non-uniform) charge distribution on the long wire can be found by考虑到 the charge density \(\lambda\) is uniform along the wire. The electric field due to the wire at distance \(r\) from the wire is given by:

\[
E = \frac{\lambda}{2\pi \epsilon_0 r}
\]

For \(r = 1.5 \, \text{cm} = 0.015 \, \text{m}\) and \(\lambda = 3.6 \, \text{nC/m} = 3.6 \times 10^{-9} \, \text{C/m}\), the electric field is:

\[
E = \frac{3.6 \times 10^{-9}}{2 \pi (8.85 \times 10^{-12}) \cdot 0.015} \approx \frac{3.6 \times 10^{-9}}{0.001047 \, \text{m}^2}
\]

The electric field due to the charge on the cylindrical shell can be calculated as:

\[
E_{\text{shell}} = \frac{\sigma}{\epsilon_0}
\]

To make the net external electric field zero, \(E + E_{\text{shell}} = 0\:

\[
\frac{3.6 \times 10^{-9}}{0.001047} + \frac{\sigma}{8.85 \times 10^{-12}} = 0
\]

To find \(\sigma\), rearrange the equation:

\[
\sigma = -\frac{3.6 \times 10^{-9}}{0.001047} \cdot 8.85 \times 10^{-12}
\]

The answer is因此 \(\sigma \approx \frac{3.6 \times 8.85 \times 10^{-12}}{0.001047} \approx \frac{31.86 \times 10^{-12}}{0.001047} \approx 30.42 \times 10^{-12} \, \text{C/m}^2\)。

The answer is因此 \(\boxed{30.42 \times 10^{-12}}\).

\[
F = qE
\]

where \( F \) is the force, \( q \) is the charge of the proton, and \( E \) is the electric field strength. The charge of a proton is \( q = 1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C} \).

1. **Calculate the force on the proton**:

\[
F = qE = (1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}) \times (2.00 \times 10^4 \, \text{N/C}) = 3.204 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{N}
\]

2. **recall the formula for acceleration**:

\[
a = \frac{F}{m}
\]

where \( m \) is the mass of the proton, which is approximately \( m = 1.672 \times 10^{-27} \, \text{kg} \).

3. **Calculate the acceleration**:

\[
a = \frac{3.204 \times 10^{-15} \, \text{N}}{1.672 \times 10^{-27} \, \text{kg}} \approx 1.915 \times 10^{12} \, \text{m/s}^2
\]

The answer is因此 \boxed{1915000000.000} \, \text{m/s}^2.

\[

\[

1. **Calculate the volume of the rod**: 
   \[
   V = \text{ length} \times \text{ cross-sectional area} = 2.00 \, \text{m} \times 4.00 \times 10^{-4} \, \text{m}^2 = 8.00 \times 10^{-4} \, \text{m}^3
   \]

2. **Calculate the charge on the rod**: 
   \[
   Q = \rho \cdot V = -4.00 \times 10^{-6} \, \text{C/m}^3 \cdot 8.00 \times 10^{-4} \, \text{m}^3 = -3.20 \times 10^{-9} \, \text{C}
   \]

3. **Calculate the number of electrons**: 
   The charge of one electron is \( e = 1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C} \). 
   \[
   N = \frac{Q}{e} = \frac{-3.20 \times 10^{-9} \, \text{C}}{1.602 \times 10^{-19} \, \text{C}} \approx 2.00 \times 10^{10}
   \]

The answer is因此 \boxed{2.000 \times 10^{10}}.
